{'A': 'A-I, B-III, C-IV, D-II', 'B': 'A-III, B-IV, C-I, D-II', 'C': 'A-II, B-IV, C-III, D-I', 'D': 'A-III, B-I, C-II, D-IV'}
B

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 18.994em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.763em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.6%; padding: 0.897em 0px 0.239em; width: 59px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2"><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 21.819em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c59"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 53px;">&nbsp;Stress&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut <h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">(A) Planck's constant<br><br>

(D) Momentum (p) = F.t<br><br>

<br><br>A-III, B-IV, C-II, D-I</div>


<p>Given below are two statements : One is labelled as Assertion (A) and other is labelled as Reason (R).</p>
<p>Assertion (A) : Time period of oscillation of a liquid drop depends on surface tension (S), if density of the liquid is <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; 0.373em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70C TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msup><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c53"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-texatom size="s" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mn <p>Reason (R) : Using dimensional analysis we get R.H.S. having different dimension than that of time period.</p>

D

<h2 class="my-2.5 text-lg text-blue-500 font-bold svelte-1pnvkqi">Explanation</h2> <div class="question xl:text-lg mt-2">We know,

data-mjx-texclass="OPEN">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo data-mjx-texclass="CLOSE">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msup><msup><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi></mrow><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mfrac><mn>6</mn><mn>4</mn></mfrac></mrow></msup><mo data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mn>0</mn></mrow></msup><msup><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi></mrow><mrow <br><br>dimension of L.H.S. = <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c54"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>
<br><br><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2234 TEX-A"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> Dimension of LHS <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2260"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>≠</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> Dimension of RHS.</div>


<p>A travelling microscope has 20 divisions per <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c63"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi data-mjx-auto-op="false">cm</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> on the main scale while its vernier scale has total 50 divisions and 25 vernier scale divisions are equal to 24 main scale divisions, what is the least count of the travelling microscope?</p>
{'A': '0.001 cm', 'B': '0.002 mm', 'C': '0.002 cm', 'D': '0.005 cm'}
C

<p>(B) Total divisions on circular scale <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c35"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>=</mo><mn>50</mn></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></p>
<p>(C) Main scale reading is <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c2E"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c35"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 4px;">&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>2.5</mn><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi data-mjx-auto-op="false">mm</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></p>
<p>(D) <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 119.5%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msup><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c34"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c35"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.404em;"><mjx-texatom size="s" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mtext style="font-family: MJXZERO, Roboto, &quot;Tiro Bangla&quot;, &quot;Tiro Devanagari Hindi&quot;, sans-serif;"><mjx-utext variant="-explicitFont" style="font-size: 83.7%; padding: 0.896em 0px 0.239em; width: 18px;">th&nbsp;</mjx-utext></mjx-mtext></mjx-texatom></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msup><mn>45</mn><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mtext>th&nbsp;</mtext></mrow></msup></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> division of circular scale is in the pitch line</p>
<p>(E) Instrument has 0.03 mm negative error</p>
<p>Then the diameter of wire is :</p>
{'A': '2.92 mm', 'B': '2.54 mm', 'C': '2.98 mm', 'D': '3.45 mm'}
